{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_015mm2BzWzGTU9xytDVcDGuY","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01LvjgcwPTUhmcUjp7y1vDK9","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Envoy HTTP Connection Manager Architecture\n\n## Overview\n\nThe Envoy HTTP Connection Manager (HCM) is a sophisticated network filter that handles the complete lifecycle of HTTP requests flowing through a proxy. It sits at the intersection of downstream connections (client to Envoy) and upstream connections (Envoy to backend services), orchestrating the flow of data through multiple processing stages including codec translation, filter chains, routing, and request forwarding.\n\nThis document describes how the four major components—**ConnectionManagerImpl**, **FilterManager**, **Router Filter**, and **Cluster Manager**—work together to transform incoming HTTP requests into upstream communications and responses back to clients.\n\n---\n\n## Component 1: ConnectionManagerImpl — The Central Network Filter\n\n### Location\n- **Interface**: `envoy/http/api_listener.h` (defines `ServerConnectionCallbacks`)\n- **Implementation**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h` and `.cc`\n- **Configuration**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h`\n\n### Role and Responsibilities\n\n`ConnectionManagerImpl` is the central orchestrator that:\n1. Implements `Network::ReadFilter` to receive raw bytes from downstream connections\n2. Creates and manages `ActiveStream` objects for each HTTP request\n3. Instantiates and manages codecs for different HTTP protocols (HTTP/1.1, HTTP/2, HTTP/3)\n4. Handles connection-level lifecycle decisions (drain, keep-alive, overload management)\n5. Manages flow control through watermark-based buffering\n\n### Connection Lifecycle: From Bytes to Streams\n\nWhen a downstream connection arrives:\n\n```\nNetwork Layer (raw TCP/SSL)\n         ↓\nConnectionManagerImpl::onNewConnection()\n    - Initializes read filter callbacks\n    - May trigger codec creation for HTTP/3\n         ↓\nConnectionManagerImpl::onData(Buffer&, bool end_stream)\n    - Receives raw HTTP bytes\n    - Lazily creates codec if not yet created (HTTP/1.1, HTTP/2)\n    - Passes bytes to codec for parsing\n         ↓\nCodec (HTTP1::CodecImpl, HTTP2::CodecImpl, HTTP3::CodecImpl)\n    - Parses HTTP protocol-specific framing\n    - Invokes ServerConnectionCallbacks for each logical stream\n         ↓\nConnectionManagerImpl::newStream() [ServerConnectionCallbacks]\n    - Creates ResponseEncoder for the stream\n    - Returns RequestDecoder that feeds into ActiveStream\n```\n\n### ActiveStream: Per-Stream State Management\n\n**Location**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h` (nested struct within ConnectionManagerImpl)\n\nEach HTTP request/stream is wrapped in an `ActiveStream` which:\n- Implements `RequestDecoder` to receive decoded HTTP frames (headers, data, trailers, metadata)\n- Owns a `FilterManager` that manages the request/response filter chain\n- Tracks stream-specific state: routing decision, upstream request, timers, retry state\n- Implements multiple callback interfaces to handle events from codecs and filters\n- Implements `RouteCache` to cache route lookups for the stream lifetime\n\n**Key ActiveStream Responsibilities**:\n```cpp\nActiveStream:\n  - Receives: decodeHeaders(), decodeData(), decodeTrailers(), decodeMetadata()\n  - Routes to FilterManager for filter chain processing\n  - Manages stream-level timers (request timeout, per-try timeout)\n  - Delegates encoding to FilterManager (which writes to response_encoder_)\n  - Coordinates completion and logging when stream finishes\n```\n\n### Codec Instantiation Strategy\n\nEnvoy uses **lazy codec creation** for efficiency:\n\n- **HTTP/3**: Created in `onNewConnection()` because the QUIC transport setup must happen immediately\n- **HTTP/1.1 and HTTP/2**: Created in `onData()` on first data arrival, allowing the connection to remain codec-agnostic until needed\n\n**Key Files**:\n- `source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.h` — HTTP/1.1 parser and serializer\n- `source/common/http/http2/codec_impl.h` — HTTP/2 framing with stream multiplexing\n- `source/common/quic/codec_impl.h` — HTTP/3 over QUIC\n\n### Connection-Level Concerns\n\n#### Drain and Connection Closure\nWhen the listener signals drain (graceful shutdown):\n- `ConnectionManagerImpl` stops accepting new streams\n- Existing streams complete normally\n- Connection closes after last stream finishes or timeout occurs\n\n**Related Code**: `drain_close_` field and `shouldDrainConnections()` logic\n\n#### Overload Management\nThe connection manager integrates with `OverloadManager` to handle server overload:\n- **LoadShedPoint::HcmDecodeHeaders**: Sheds new requests if overload is active\n- **OverloadAction::StopAcceptingRequests**: Prevents new streams from starting\n- **OverloadAction::DisableHttpKeepAlive**: Forces connection close to reduce resource usage\n\n**Related Code**:\n- `overload_manager_` field\n- `accept_new_http_stream_` load shed point\n- `overload_stop_accepting_requests_ref_`, `overload_disable_keepalive_ref_`\n\n#### Watermark-Based Flow Control\nDownstream connection writes (upstream responses returning to client) are buffered with watermarks:\n- When the write buffer exceeds high watermark, the upstream codec pauses reading upstream responses\n- When buffer drops below low watermark, reading resumes\n- This prevents memory exhaustion if the client is slow to consume responses\n\n**Related Code**:\n- `onAboveWriteBufferHighWatermark()` / `onBelowWriteBufferLowWatermark()` callbacks\n- Propagated to codec via `ConnectionCallbacks` interface\n- Per-stream buffering through `WatermarkBuffer`\n\n---\n\n## Component 2: FilterManager and the HTTP Filter Chain\n\n### Location\n- **Core Interface**: `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`\n- **Implementation**: `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`\n\n### Architecture: Dual-Direction Filter Chains\n\nThe HTTP filter chain is **bidirectional**: filters are organized in a **decoder chain** (request direction) and an **encoder chain** (response direction).\n\n```\nDecoder Chain (Request Path):\n  Request Headers → [FilterA.decodeHeaders] → [FilterB.decodeHeaders] → ... → Router\n  Request Data    → [FilterA.decodeData]    → [FilterB.decodeData]    → ... → Router\n  Trailers        → [FilterA.decodeTrailers] → [FilterB.decodeTrailers] → ... → Router\n\nEncoder Chain (Response Path):\n  Response Headers ← [FilterC.encodeHeaders] ← [FilterB.encodeHeaders] ← [FilterA.encodeHeaders] ← Upstream/Local\n  Response Data    ← [FilterC.encodeData]    ← [FilterB.encodeData]    ← [FilterA.encodeData]    ← Upstream/Local\n  Trailers         ← [FilterC.encodeTrailers] ← [FilterB.encodeTrailers] ← [FilterA.encodeTrailers] ← Upstream/Local\n```\n\n**Key Design Decision**: Encoder filters iterate in **reverse order** of their configuration. This ensures symmetric request/response processing: a filter that modifies headers on the way down modifies them on the way back in reverse order.\n\n### Filter Chain Execution Engine\n\n#### Decoder Filter Chain Iteration\n\nWhen `ActiveStream` receives decoded headers from the codec:\n\n```cpp\nActiveStream::decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMapSharedPtr&& headers, bool end_stream)\n  ↓\nFilterManager::decodeHeaders(headers, end_stream)\n  ↓\nFor each decoder filter in sequence:\n  - Call filter->decodeHeaders(headers, end_stream)\n  - Based on return status:\n    ✓ FilterHeadersStatus::Continue → Proceed to next filter\n    ✗ FilterHeadersStatus::StopIteration → Stop chain, wait for continueDecoding()\n    ✗ FilterHeadersStatus::StopAllIterationAndBuffer → Stop and buffer body data\n    ✗ FilterHeadersStatus::StopAllIterationAndWatermark → Stop, buffer, and apply watermarks\n```\n\nEach filter wrapper (`ActiveStreamDecoderFilter`) stores:\n- **Filter instance** (`StreamDecoderFilterSharedPtr handle_`)\n- **Iteration state** (Continue, StopSingleIteration, StopAllBuffer, StopAllWatermark)\n- **Buffered data** if iteration stopped\n\n**Key Data Structures**:\n- `StreamDecoderFilters` — vector of `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter` pointers\n- `StreamEncoderFilters` — vector of `ActiveStreamEncoderFilter` pointers (with reverse iterator)\n- `FilterContext` — metadata about the filter including its config name for debugging\n\n#### Encoder Filter Chain Iteration\n\nEncoding follows the same pattern but iterates encoder filters in **reverse**:\n\n```cpp\nFilterManager::encodeHeaders(ResponseHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream)\n  ↓\nFor each encoder filter in reverse sequence:\n  - Call filter->encodeHeaders(headers, end_stream)\n  - Based on return status: Continue or StopIteration\n  - Stop → Wait for continueEncoding()\n```\n\nThis reverse iteration ensures that if filter A modifies a response header, filter B's encoding (applied after filter A's) operates on the modified header.\n\n### Filter Factory and Creation\n\n**Location**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h` (nested factory logic)\n\nWhen `ActiveStream` is created:\n```cpp\nActiveStream::ActiveStream(ConnectionManagerImpl& parent, ...)\n  ↓\nFilterManager::FilterManager(...)\n  ↓\nFor each configured HTTP filter in config_.http_filters:\n  - Obtain FilterFactoryCallbacks for the filter\n  - Call factory->createFilterFactoryFromProto() to instantiate filter\n  - Call setFilterFactoryCallbacks() to set callbacks\n  - Store in either decoder or encoder (or both for StreamFilter) vectors\n```\n\n### Filter Types and Their Roles\n\nEnvoy provides three filter base classes:\n\n1. **`StreamDecoderFilter`** — Processes requests only\n   ```cpp\n   class StreamDecoderFilter {\n     virtual FilterHeadersStatus decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMap&, bool end_stream) PURE;\n     virtual FilterDataStatus decodeData(Buffer::Instance&, bool end_stream) PURE;\n     virtual FilterTrailersStatus decodeTrailers(RequestTrailerMap&) PURE;\n     virtual void setDecoderFilterCallbacks(StreamDecoderFilterCallbacks&) PURE;\n   };\n   ```\n\n2. **`StreamEncoderFilter`** — Processes responses only\n   ```cpp\n   class StreamEncoderFilter {\n     virtual Filter1xxHeadersStatus encode1xxHeaders(ResponseHeaderMap&) PURE;\n     virtual FilterHeadersStatus encodeHeaders(ResponseHeaderMap&, bool end_stream) PURE;\n     virtual FilterDataStatus encodeData(Buffer::Instance&, bool end_stream) PURE;\n     virtual FilterTrailersStatus encodeTrailers(ResponseTrailerMap&) PURE;\n     virtual void setEncoderFilterCallbacks(StreamEncoderFilterCallbacks&) PURE;\n   };\n   ```\n\n3. **`StreamFilter`** — Bidirectional filter (inherits from both `StreamDecoderFilter` and `StreamEncoderFilter`)\n   ```cpp\n   class StreamFilter : public virtual StreamDecoderFilter,\n                        public virtual StreamEncoderFilter { };\n   ```\n\n### Filter Control Flow: StopIteration Semantics\n\nWhen a filter returns `FilterHeadersStatus::StopIteration`:\n- The filter chain halts before the next filter\n- The current filter is responsible for resuming iteration via `continueDecoding()` or `continueEncoding()`\n- Common use case: **Router Filter** returns `StopIteration` to wait for upstream response before passing headers downstream\n\nWhen a filter returns `FilterHeadersStatus::StopAllIterationAndBuffer`:\n- Iteration stops for all remaining filters\n- Incoming body data is buffered in memory\n- The filter must eventually call `continueDecoding()` to resume\n- Used by filters that need to inspect or modify the complete body before forwarding\n\n### Filter Callbacks: Bidirectional Communication\n\n#### `StreamDecoderFilterCallbacks`\nAllows decoder filters to communicate back to the connection manager:\n```cpp\nclass StreamDecoderFilterCallbacks : public virtual StreamFilterCallbacks {\n  // Routing\n  virtual Router::RouteConstSharedPtr route() PURE;\n\n  // Upstream connection handling\n  virtual Upstream::ClusterInfoConstSharedPtr clusterInfo() PURE;\n\n  // Local responses (bypass upstream)\n  virtual void sendLocalReply(Code code, absl::string_view body,\n                              const std::function<void(ResponseHeaderMap&)>& modify_headers,\n                              const absl::optional<Grpc::Status::GrpcStatus> grpc_status,\n                              absl::string_view details) PURE;\n\n  // Flow control\n  virtual void setBufferLimit(uint64_t limit) PURE;\n\n  // Continuing iteration\n  virtual void continueDecoding() PURE;\n};\n```\n\n#### `StreamEncoderFilterCallbacks`\nAllows encoder filters to interact with upstream information:\n```cpp\nclass StreamEncoderFilterCallbacks : public virtual StreamFilterCallbacks {\n  // Upstream request state\n  virtual OptRef<const Upstream::HostDescription> upstreamHost() PURE;\n\n  // Flow control\n  virtual void continueEncoding() PURE;\n};\n```\n\n#### Common `StreamFilterCallbacks`\nBoth decoder and encoder filters inherit this base:\n```cpp\nclass StreamFilterCallbacks {\n  // Connection and stream info\n  virtual const Network::Connection* connection() PURE;\n  virtual uint64_t streamId() const PURE;\n  virtual StreamInfo::StreamInfo& streamInfo() PURE;\n\n  // Tracing\n  virtual Tracing::Span& activeSpan() PURE;\n\n  // Routing\n  virtual Router::RouteConstSharedPtr route() PURE;\n  virtual const Router::RouteSpecificFilterConfig* mostSpecificPerFilterConfig() const PURE;\n\n  // Reset handling\n  virtual void resetStream(Http::StreamResetReason reset_reason,\n                          absl::string_view transport_failure_reason) PURE;\n\n  // Dispatcher for async operations\n  virtual Event::Dispatcher& dispatcher() PURE;\n};\n```\n\n### Filter Manager Internals\n\n**Location**: `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`\n\nThe `FilterManager` class maintains:\n- **Request/response headers and trailers** (`RequestHeaderMapSharedPtr`, `ResponseHeaderMapSharedPtr`)\n- **Decoder and encoder filter vectors** (`StreamDecoderFilters`, `StreamEncoderFilters`)\n- **Stream information** for tracking request/response state\n- **Active span** for distributed tracing\n- **Route cache** to avoid repeated route lookups\n\n#### Metadata Handling\n\nHTTP/2 and HTTP/3 support **metadata frames**. When a filter stops iteration, metadata can be buffered:\n- `SavedRequestMetadata_` — holds metadata frames that arrived before a decoder filter resumed\n- `SavedResponseMetadata_` — holds metadata frames that arrived before an encoder filter resumed\n\nWhen iteration resumes, buffered metadata is replayed to the next filter.\n\n---\n\n## Component 3: Router Filter — Terminal Decoder Filter for Upstream Dispatch\n\n### Location\n- **Interface**: `envoy/router/router.h`\n- **Implementation**: `source/common/router/router.cc` and associated files\n- **Configuration Factory**: `source/common/router/config_impl.h` and `config_utility.h`\n\n### Role and Responsibilities\n\nThe Router Filter is the **last decoder filter in the chain**. It:\n1. **Selects a route** using `RouteConfiguration` based on request headers/path\n2. **Obtains an upstream connection pool** from `ClusterManager` for the selected cluster\n3. **Creates an upstream request** and manages its lifecycle\n4. **Implements retry logic** based on route policy and response codes\n5. **Handles hedged requests** (concurrent upstream attempts)\n6. **Manages timeouts** at multiple levels (global, per-try, per-try-idle)\n7. **Implements shadow routing** for sending traffic to alternate clusters\n\n### Route Selection\n\nWhen `Router::decodeHeaders()` is called:\n\n```cpp\nRouter::Filter::decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream)\n  ↓\ncallbacks_->route()  // Obtain Route from RouterConfig\n  ↓\nRouteEntry route = route_->routeEntry()  // Get destination cluster and settings\n  ↓\ncluster_ = cluster_manager_.clusters().get(route->clusterName())\n```\n\n**Route Matching Process**:\n1. HTTP path and method matched against configured `VirtualHost` patterns\n2. `RouteEntry` provides:\n   - Cluster name (backend destination)\n   - Timeout policy\n   - Retry policy\n   - Load balancer metadata\n   - Header manipulations (add/remove/append)\n   - Redirect rules\n\n**Key Files**:\n- `source/common/router/config_impl.h` — RouteConfiguration and RouteEntry implementation\n- `source/common/router/matcher_visitor.h` — Route matching logic\n\n### Upstream Connection Pool Acquisition\n\nThe router obtains a **connection pool** per upstream cluster:\n\n```cpp\nRouter::Filter::decodeHeaders(...)\n  ↓\nUpstream::ThreadLocalCluster tlc = cluster_manager_.getThreadLocalCluster(cluster_name)\n  ↓\nHttp::ConnectionPool::Instance* pool =\n    tlc->httpConnPool(priority, protocol, downstream_connection)\n  ↓\nConnectionPool obtained for the specific:\n  - Cluster\n  - Resource Priority (default, high, medium, low)\n  - HTTP Protocol (auto-selected or overridden)\n  - Socket options (source IP, TLS settings, etc.)\n```\n\n**Connection Pool Responsibilities**:\n- Maintains a pool of **physical TCP/TLS connections** to the upstream host\n- **Multiplexes multiple HTTP requests** over HTTP/2 connections\n- **Reuses connections** from the pool when available\n- **Creates new connections** when pool is exhausted or no idle connections remain\n- **Handles connection failures** and triggers host health updates\n\n### UpstreamRequest Lifecycle\n\nWhen the router has a connection pool and is ready to send upstream:\n\n```cpp\nstruct UpstreamRequest {\n  // Created by Router::startUpstreamRequest()\n\n  // Identifying information\n  uint32_t upstream_request_id_;\n  Router::Filter* parent_;  // Back-reference to router filter\n  Http::ResponseDecoder response_decoder_;  // Decodes upstream responses\n\n  // Connection pool callback\n  Http::ConnectionPool::Callbacks pool_callbacks_;\n\n  // Upstream stream and encoder\n  Http::StreamEncoderPtr request_encoder_;  // Encodes request to upstream\n  Http::RequestHeaderMapPtr upstream_headers_;\n\n  // Timers\n  Event::TimerPtr per_try_timeout_timer_;\n  Event::TimerPtr per_try_idle_timer_;\n\n  // State\n  bool started_;\n  bool decode_complete_;  // All response received?\n  bool awaiting_headers_;\n};\n```\n\n### Upstream Request Execution\n\n```cpp\n1. Encode request headers to upstream via request_encoder_->encodeHeaders()\n\n2. If there's a request body, stream it via request_encoder_->encodeData()\n\n3. Upstream codec parses response and calls response_decoder_->decodeHeaders()\n\n4. Router processes response headers:\n   - Applies header transformations (response_entry->finalizeResponseHeaders())\n   - Checks for retry eligibility if response indicates failure\n   - If retryable, goto Step 5; otherwise proceed to Step 6\n\n5. If retrying:\n   - Destroy current UpstreamRequest\n   - Decrement retry counter\n   - Go back to connection pool acquisition (Step 2)\n\n6. Send response headers downstream via encoder_->encodeHeaders()\n\n7. Stream response body downstream via encoder_->encodeData()\n\n8. Stream response trailers downstream via encoder_->encodeTrailers()\n```\n\n### Retry Logic\n\n**Location**: `source/common/router/retry_state_impl.h` and `.cc`\n\nRetries are controlled by:\n1. **Route retry policy** — defines which conditions trigger retries\n2. **Request headers** — can override route policy via `x-envoy-retry-on`, `x-envoy-max-retries`\n3. **Response status code** — certain 5xx codes and connection errors trigger retries\n\n```cpp\nRetryPolicy retry_conditions = {\n  RETRY_ON_5XX,                    // 500-599 status codes\n  RETRY_ON_GATEWAY_ERROR,          // 502, 503, 504\n  RETRY_ON_CONNECT_FAILURE,        // Connection reset, refused\n  RETRY_ON_RETRIABLE_4XX,          // 409, 429\n  RETRY_ON_RESET,                  // Stream reset\n  RETRY_ON_REFUSED_STREAM,         // HTTP/2 refused stream\n  // ... and others\n};\n```\n\nWhen a retryable condition is detected:\n- Current upstream request is destroyed\n- Upstream connection pool releases the request\n- New upstream request attempts the next host (via load balancing) or same host\n- Per-try timeout is reset for the new attempt\n\n**Maximum Retries**: Limited by route policy and `x-envoy-max-retries` header\n\n### Timeout Handling\n\nThe router implements **three levels of timeouts**:\n\n#### 1. Global Timeout\nThe entire request lifecycle from decoding headers to receiving final response:\n```cpp\nTimeoutData timeout = FilterUtility::finalTimeout(route, headers, ...);\nstd::chrono::milliseconds global_timeout = timeout.global_timeout_;\n\n// Set timer\nglobal_timeout_timer_ = dispatcher.createTimer([this]() {\n  onUpstreamTimeoutAbort(...);  // Send 504 downstream\n});\n```\n\n#### 2. Per-Try Timeout\nIndividual upstream attempt timeout, independent of retries:\n```cpp\nstd::chrono::milliseconds per_try_timeout = timeout.per_try_timeout_;\n\nupstream_request->per_try_timeout_timer_ = dispatcher.createTimer([this]() {\n  onPerTryTimeout(*upstream_request);  // Retry if eligible\n});\n```\n\n#### 3. Per-Try Idle Timeout\nTimeout if no data flows for a period during a single attempt:\n```cpp\nupstream_request->per_try_idle_timer_ = dispatcher.createTimer([this]() {\n  onPerTryIdleTimeout(*upstream_request);  // Retry or fail\n});\n```\n\nThe timer in **Configuration**:\n- Specified in route config (`timeout`, `per_try_timeout`)\n- Can be overridden by request header `x-envoy-upstream-rq-timeout-ms`\n\n### Hedged Requests\n\n**Location**: `source/common/router/router.cc` (hedging logic in `Filter::startUpstreamRequest()`)\n\nHedged requests allow **concurrent upstream attempts** to reduce tail latency:\n\n```\nInitial request attempt:\n  Send to upstream host A with per-try-timeout of 100ms\n\nIf no response after 80ms AND hedge is enabled:\n  Launch second concurrent attempt to upstream host B\n\nWhichever upstream responds first wins:\n  - Response passed downstream\n  - Other attempt canceled (reset)\n  - Upstream connection returned to pool\n```\n\n**Configuration**:\n- Route-level hedge policy: `hedge_policy.hedge_on_per_try_timeout`\n- Header override: `x-envoy-hedge-on-per-try-timeout`\n\n### Shadow Routing\n\n**Location**: `source/common/router/router.cc` (shadow routing in `Filter::decodeHeaders()`)\n\nShadow routing sends **read-only copies** of requests to alternate clusters for traffic analysis:\n\n```cpp\n// After selecting primary route and cluster\nfor (const auto& shadow_policy : route->shadowPolicies()) {\n  // Determine if we should shadow this request\n  if (FilterUtility::shouldShadow(shadow_policy, random)) {\n    // Create separate upstream request to shadow cluster\n    // Send request data\n    // Discard response (don't affect client)\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Key Properties**:\n- Shadow requests are **not retried**\n- Shadow responses are **not sent to client**\n- Used for canary testing, traffic shadowing, A/B testing\n- Controlled by `x-envoy-shadowed-header` to avoid infinite loops\n\n### Response Processing\n\nWhen upstream response headers arrive:\n\n```cpp\nUpstreamRequest::decodeHeaders(ResponseHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream)\n  ↓\nRouter::Filter::onUpstreamResponse(...)\n  ↓\n1. Check if response is retryable (e.g., 503)\n2. If retry eligible and retries remaining: trigger retry (goto new attempt)\n3. Otherwise:\n   - Apply response header transformations\n   - Update stream info with upstream details\n   - Call parent_->encoder_->encodeHeaders() to send to client\n   - If end_stream=true, response complete\n   - Otherwise, prepare to receive body data\n```\n\n---\n\n## Component 4: Cluster Manager and Upstream Connectivity\n\n### Location\n- **Interface**: `envoy/upstream/cluster_manager.h`\n- **Implementation**: `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h` and `.cc`\n- **Connection Pools**: `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.h`, `http1/conn_pool.h`, `http2/conn_pool.h`\n\n### ClusterManager: The Upstream Abstraction\n\n`ClusterManager` is Envoy's **central registry of upstream clusters**. It:\n1. Manages configuration of all upstream clusters\n2. Provides thread-local cluster instances for zero-lock access\n3. Creates and caches connection pools per cluster/host pair\n4. Coordinates health checking and load balancing\n5. Provides statistics and observability\n\n### Obtaining a Thread-Local Cluster\n\nFor thread safety without locks, Envoy uses **thread-local storage**:\n\n```cpp\n// In router filter (on Envoy's event dispatcher thread)\nUpstream::ThreadLocalCluster* tlc =\n    cluster_manager_.getThreadLocalCluster(cluster_name);\n\n// ThreadLocalCluster wraps:\n// - Cluster config (name, health checker, circuit breaker limits)\n// - Load balancer instance\n// - Connection pool map\n// - Host priority list\n```\n\nEach **event dispatcher thread** has its own thread-local cluster instance, eliminating lock contention.\n\n### Cluster and Host Hierarchy\n\n```\nCluster\n├── PriorityLevel 0\n│   ├── Host A (address 10.0.1.1:8080)\n│   ├── Host B (address 10.0.1.2:8080)\n│   └── Host C (address 10.0.1.3:8080)\n├── PriorityLevel 1\n│   └── Host D (address 10.0.2.1:8080)\n└── ...\n```\n\nEach **Host** tracks:\n- Network address (IP/port)\n- Health status (healthy, unhealthy, unknown)\n- Connection statistics (active connections, total requests)\n- Performance data (load balancing weight, locality)\n\n### Load Balancing\n\n**Location**: `envoy/upstream/load_balancer.h`\n\nWhen the router needs to forward a request:\n\n```cpp\n// Get a specific host via load balancer\nUpstream::HostConstSharedPtr host =\n    lb_->chooseHost(load_balance_context);\n```\n\nLoad balancing **strategies** include:\n- **Round-robin** — cycle through healthy hosts\n- **Least request** — choose host with fewest active requests\n- **Ring hash** — consistent hash of headers/cookies for session stickiness\n- **Random** — random host selection\n- **Maglev** — advanced consistent hash\n\nThe load balancer consults:\n- **Health status** — skips unhealthy hosts\n- **Request context** — metadata for sticky sessions\n- **Statistics** — active connections, request counts\n\n### Connection Pools: Logical vs. Physical Connections\n\n**Logical Connection Pool** (per-cluster):\n- Manages HTTP stream multiplexing over HTTP/2\n- Single pool handles many concurrent requests\n- Implements queue-based request scheduling if all connections busy\n\n**Physical Connection** (to specific host):\n- Underlying TCP or TLS connection to upstream\n- HTTP/1.1: One physical connection = one request at a time\n- HTTP/2: One physical connection = many concurrent requests (multiplexed)\n- HTTP/3: One QUIC connection = many concurrent streams\n\n```\nHttp::ConnectionPool::Instance\n├── ActiveConnection (HTTP/1.1)\n│   ├── CodecClient → HttpCodecImpl\n│   └── Physical socket\n├── ActiveConnection (HTTP/2)\n│   ├── CodecClient → HTTP2CodecImpl\n│   ├── Multiplexed Stream A\n│   ├── Multiplexed Stream B\n│   └── Physical socket\n└── PendingStream queue (if all connections busy)\n```\n\n### Connection Pool Request Flow\n\nWhen router submits request to connection pool:\n\n```cpp\nHttp::ConnectionPool::Cancellable* cancellable = pool->newStream(\n    upstream_request->response_decoder_,\n    upstream_request->pool_callbacks_,\n    stream_options\n);\n\n// Pool either:\n// 1. Has idle connection → Immediately calls callbacks->onPoolReady()\n// 2. Has available multiplexing capacity → Create new stream, onPoolReady()\n// 3. No capacity, queue pending → Waits for available capacity\n// 4. Cannot connect → Calls callbacks->onPoolFailure()\n```\n\n### Connection Pool Callbacks\n\nWhen pool decides on an action:\n\n```cpp\nstruct Http::ConnectionPool::Callbacks {\n  // Pool successfully allocated a stream\n  void onPoolReady(RawAsyncStream& async_stream,\n                   UpstreamHost& upstream_host);\n\n  // Pool could not allocate (all connections exhausted, host down, etc.)\n  void onPoolFailure(PoolFailureReason reason,\n                     absl::string_view failure_reason,\n                     UpstreamHostDescription& upstream_host);\n};\n```\n\n**Router's implementation**:\n- `onPoolReady()` → Encodes request headers via stream encoder\n- `onPoolFailure()` → Checks retry eligibility, retries or sends error downstream\n\n### Circuit Breaking and Overload\n\n**Location**: `envoy/upstream/resource_manager.h`\n\nClusters enforce **circuit breaker limits**:\n```cpp\nCircuitBreakerStats limits {\n  max_connections: 100,      // Max concurrent connections to cluster\n  max_pending_requests: 100,  // Max queued requests\n  max_requests: 100,          // Max concurrent active requests\n  max_retries: 100,           // Max concurrent retry attempts\n};\n```\n\nIf limits exceeded:\n- Connection pool returns `onPoolFailure()`\n- Router checks if retry is allowed (doesn't consume retry budget)\n- If not retriable, returns 503 to client\n\n### Health Checking and Outlier Detection\n\n**Location**: `envoy/upstream/health_check_host_monitor.h`\n\nClusters maintain **health status** updated by:\n\n1. **Active Health Checking** — Periodic probes to upstream hosts\n   - If probe fails → Mark unhealthy\n   - Load balancer skips unhealthy hosts\n\n2. **Outlier Detection** — Passive monitoring of request failures\n   - Tracks error rates, latencies, consecutive errors\n   - Ejects underperforming hosts (temporarily)\n   - Periodically re-admits ejected hosts\n\nWhen a host becomes unhealthy:\n- Load balancer routes to healthy alternatives\n- Failing requests may be retried to healthy hosts\n\n### Connection Pool Mechanics: HTTP/1.1 vs HTTP/2\n\n#### HTTP/1.1 Connection Pool\n```\nOne request per physical connection:\n\nRequest 1 → Connection A → Upstream\nRequest 2 → Connection B → Upstream\nRequest 3 → Queue (waiting for Connection A or B to free up)\n\nWhen Connection A response completes:\n  Dequeue Request 3\n  Reuse Connection A for Request 3\n```\n\n#### HTTP/2 Connection Pool\n```\nMultiple requests per physical connection (multiplexed):\n\nRequest 1 ┐\nRequest 2 ├→ Connection A (single physical socket, multiple HTTP/2 streams)\nRequest 3 ┘\nRequest 4 ─→ Connection B (second physical socket if pool limit reached)\n\nEach request gets a unique HTTP/2 stream ID within the connection\n```\n\n---\n\n## Data Flow: Request from Bytes to Upstream and Back\n\nThis section traces a complete request lifecycle through all four components.\n\n### **Phase 1: Bytes Arrive at Downstream Connection**\n\n```\n1. TCP socket receives HTTP bytes from client\n                ↓\n2. Network layer invokes ConnectionManagerImpl::onData(Buffer&, bool end_stream)\n                ↓\n3. Is codec created?\n   NO → CreateCodec (lazily create HTTP/1.1 or HTTP/2)\n                ↓\n4. Pass buffer to codec for parsing\n   codec.onData(buffer)\n                ↓\n5. Codec parses HTTP frames and invokes:\n   ServerConnectionCallbacks::newStream(ResponseEncoder&)\n```\n\n### **Phase 2: Stream Creation and Filter Chain Initialization**\n\n```\n6. ConnectionManagerImpl::newStream() [ServerConnectionCallbacks]\n                ↓\n7. Create ActiveStream(stream_id, filter_manager, ...)\n                ↓\n8. FilterManager instantiates all configured HTTP filters\n                ↓\n9. Return RequestDecoder from ActiveStream to codec\n                ↓\n10. Codec invokes RequestDecoder::decodeHeaders(headers, end_stream)\n```\n\n### **Phase 3: Request Flows Through Decoder Chain**\n\n```\n11. ActiveStream::decodeHeaders()\n                ↓\n12. FilterManager::decodeHeaders()\n                ↓\n13. Iterate decoder filters:\n    For each filter in config order:\n      - filter.decodeHeaders(headers, end_stream)\n      - If StopIteration: halt, wait for continueDecoding()\n      - If Continue: proceed to next filter\n                ↓\n14. Last filter = Router Filter\n                ↓\n15. Router::decodeHeaders():\n      a) callbacks_->route() to get RouteEntry\n      b) Extract cluster name from route\n      c) Get connection pool from cluster_manager_\n      d) Submit request to connection pool\n      e) Return StopIteration (wait for upstream response)\n```\n\n### **Phase 4: Upstream Request Execution**\n\n```\n16. Connection pool either:\n    - Returns idle connection → onPoolReady() immediately\n    - Creates new connection and calls onPoolReady()\n    - Queues pending stream if no capacity available\n                ↓\n17. Router::onPoolReady(request_encoder)\n                ↓\n18. Encode request headers:\n    request_encoder->encodeHeaders(upstream_headers, end_stream=false)\n                ↓\n19. If client request has body:\n    codec.onData() → ActiveStream::decodeData()\n                ↓\n20. FilterManager::decodeData()\n                ↓\n21. Router::decodeData() (typically passes through)\n                ↓\n22. Router forwards to upstream:\n    request_encoder->encodeData(buffer, end_stream=false)\n                ↓\n23. If client request has trailers:\n    codec.onTrailers() → ActiveStream::decodeTrailers()\n                ↓\n24. Router::decodeTrailers()\n                ↓\n25. request_encoder->encodeTrailers(trailers)\n```\n\n### **Phase 5: Upstream Response Returns**\n\n```\n26. Upstream connection receives response bytes\n                ↓\n27. Upstream codec parses response and invokes:\n    ResponseDecoder::decodeHeaders(response_headers, bool end_stream)\n                ↓\n28. Router::UpstreamRequest::decodeHeaders() (as ResponseDecoder impl)\n                ↓\n29. Router::onUpstreamResponse(response_headers)\n      a) Check if response is retryable\n      b) If retryable AND retries remaining:\n         - Cancel per-try timers\n         - Destroy current upstream request\n         - Go back to connection pool (Phase 4)\n      c) Otherwise:\n         - Update response headers (strip hop-by-hop, add routing headers)\n         - Call encoder_->encodeHeaders(response_headers, end_stream)\n                ↓\n30. FilterManager::encodeHeaders()\n                ↓\n31. Iterate encoder filters in REVERSE order:\n    For each filter (in reverse config order):\n      - filter.encodeHeaders(headers, end_stream)\n      - If StopIteration: halt, wait for continueEncoding()\n      - If Continue: proceed to previous filter\n                ↓\n32. Headers encoded to downstream connection via response_encoder\n```\n\n### **Phase 6: Response Body Flows Downstream**\n\n```\n33. Upstream continues sending body chunks:\n    Upstream codec → UpstreamRequest::decodeData()\n                ↓\n34. Router::UpstreamRequest::decodeData()\n                ↓\n35. Router forwards via:\n    encoder_->encodeData(buffer, end_stream=false)\n                ↓\n36. FilterManager::encodeData()\n                ↓\n37. Encoder filters process data (in reverse)\n                ↓\n38. Data written to downstream response_encoder\n                ↓\n39. Downstream codec serializes to TCP socket\n```\n\n### **Phase 7: Response Completion and Cleanup**\n\n```\n40. Upstream sends trailers or final chunk:\n    UpstreamRequest::decodeTrailers() or final decodeData(end_stream=true)\n                ↓\n41. Router forwards trailers:\n    encoder_->encodeTrailers(trailers)\n                ↓\n42. FilterManager::encodeTrailers()\n                ↓\n43. Downstream response_encoder finalizes response\n                ↓\n44. ConnectionManagerImpl detects response complete\n                ↓\n45. ActiveStream::completeRequest():\n    - Log request (access logs)\n    - Collect timing stats\n    - Cleanup resources\n    - Dequeue next request if pipelined (HTTP/1.1) or multiplex (HTTP/2)\n                ↓\n46. Upstream connection pool returns request to pool\n                ↓\n47. If pool has pending requests: allocate connection to next pending request\n                ↓\n48. If no pending requests: mark connection idle, reset activity timers\n```\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling Strategies\n\n### **Codec Errors**\n\nWhen the codec encounters malformed HTTP data:\n```\nHTTP/1.1 codec invalid frame\n              ↓\nCodec invokes error callback\n              ↓\nConnectionManagerImpl::onCodecError()\n              ↓\nGenerate 400 Bad Request to client\n              ↓\nClose downstream connection\n```\n\n**Stats**: `http.downstream_rq_invalid` counter incremented\n\n### **Filter Errors**\n\nIf a filter throws exception or returns error status:\n```\nFilter::decodeHeaders() throws\n              ↓\nFilterManager catches exception\n              ↓\nIf filter returned error/exception before headers sent:\n  - Generate 500 Internal Server Error (local reply)\n  - Track in stats\n\nIf filter error after headers sent:\n  - Reset stream with error code\n  - Connection may close if unrecoverable\n```\n\n**Stats**: `http.{filter_name}.error` counter\n\n### **Upstream Failures**\n\n#### Connection Pool Failure\n```\npool->newStream() → onPoolFailure()\n              ↓\nReason: No healthy hosts, circuit breaker limit, connection refused\n              ↓\nRouter checks route policy for retryability\n              ↓\nIf retryable AND retries available:\n  - Increment retry counter\n  - Attempt alternate host\n  - Go back to pool acquisition\n              ↓\nIf not retryable or retries exhausted:\n  - Generate 503 Service Unavailable\n  - Update stream info with CoreResponseFlag\n  - Send to client\n```\n\n**Stats**: `cluster.{cluster_name}.upstream_cx_connect_fail`\n\n#### Upstream Connection Reset\n```\nConnection lost mid-request\n              ↓\nUpstream codec sends stream reset\n              ↓\nRouter::UpstreamRequest::onResetStream()\n              ↓\nCheck retry policy for RETRY_ON_RESET\n              ↓\nIf retryable: retry via alternate host or same host\nIf not: send 504 Gateway Timeout or 503 Service Unavailable\n```\n\n**Stats**: `cluster.{cluster_name}.upstream_rq_reset`\n\n#### Timeout\n```\nPer-try timeout fires\n              ↓\nRouter::onPerTryTimeout()\n              ↓\nCheck if retries available\n              ↓\nIf retryable: reset upstream request, retry\nIf exhausted: send 504 Gateway Timeout\n```\n\n**Stats**: `cluster.{cluster_name}.upstream_rq_time_out`\n\n### **Local Replies**\n\nA filter can inject a response locally (bypass upstream):\n```\nFilter::decodeHeaders() calls:\n  callbacks_->sendLocalReply(Code code, body, modify_headers_fn, ...)\n              ↓\nFilterManager::sendLocalReply()\n              ↓\n1. Build response headers\n2. Invoke modify_headers_fn (for filter customization)\n3. Stop decoder iteration (don't send upstream)\n4. Encode response headers to client\n5. Encode body\n6. Mark stream as complete\n```\n\n**Common Uses**:\n- Authentication filter: 401 Unauthorized before routing\n- Rate limit filter: 429 Too Many Requests\n- Validation filter: 400 Bad Request on invalid input\n\n---\n\n## Extension Points: How to Customize Envoy\n\n### **1. HTTP Filters**\n\nCreate custom filter by implementing `StreamDecoderFilter`, `StreamEncoderFilter`, or `StreamFilter`:\n\n```cpp\n// source/extensions/filters/http/custom_filter/filter.h\nclass CustomFilter : public Http::StreamDecoderFilter {\npublic:\n  FilterHeadersStatus decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMap& headers,\n                                   bool end_stream) override;\n  FilterDataStatus decodeData(Buffer::Instance& data,\n                             bool end_stream) override;\n  void setDecoderFilterCallbacks(StreamDecoderFilterCallbacks& callbacks) override;\n\nprivate:\n  StreamDecoderFilterCallbacks* callbacks_;\n};\n\n// source/extensions/filters/http/custom_filter/config.cc\nclass CustomFilterFactory : public NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory {\npublic:\n  FilterFactoryStatus createFilter(...) override { ... }\n};\n\n// Register via:\nREGISTER_FACTORY(CustomFilterFactory, NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory);\n```\n\n### **2. Cluster Extensions**\n\nCreate custom upstream cluster type:\n\n```cpp\nclass CustomCluster : public Upstream::Cluster {\npublic:\n  // Implement cluster interface\n  virtual const Upstream::PrioritySet& prioritySet() const override;\n  virtual Upstream::HostConstSharedPtr chooseHost(LoadBalancerContext*) override;\n  // ... etc\n};\n\nclass CustomClusterFactory : public ClusterFactory {\n  CreateClusterStatus createCluster(...) override { ... }\n};\n```\n\n### **3. Load Balancers**\n\nImplement custom load balancing strategy:\n\n```cpp\nclass CustomLoadBalancer : public Upstream::LoadBalancer {\npublic:\n  // Balance method called by router\n  virtual HostConstSharedPtr chooseHost(LoadBalancerContext* context) override;\n};\n\nclass CustomLoadBalancerFactory : public Upstream::LoadBalancerFactory {\n  LoadBalancerPtr newLoadBalancer(...) override { ... }\n};\n```\n\n### **4. Access Loggers**\n\nImplement custom logging for requests:\n\n```cpp\nclass CustomAccessLog : public AccessLog::Instance {\npublic:\n  void log(const Http::RequestHeaderMap* request_headers,\n          const Http::ResponseHeaderMap* response_headers,\n          const Http::ResponseTrailerMap* response_trailers,\n          const StreamInfo::StreamInfo& stream_info) override;\n};\n```\n\n**Configured in `http_connection_manager.access_logs`**\n\n### **5. Router Filters (Advanced)**\n\nWhile most routing customization is done via `RouteEntry`, Envoy also supports:\n- **Route matcher plugins**: Custom header/path matching logic\n- **Route config providers**: Dynamic route fetching (RDS)\n- **Shadow writers**: Custom shadow request handling\n\n---\n\n## Statistics and Observability\n\n### **Connection-Level Stats** (from ConnectionManagerImpl)\n```\nhttp.downstream_cx_total           # Total downstream connections\nhttp.downstream_cx_active          # Current active connections\nhttp.downstream_cx_length_ms       # Connection lifetime histogram\nhttp.downstream_rq_total           # Total requests received\nhttp.downstream_rq_active          # Currently processing requests\nhttp.downstream_rq_time_ms         # Request processing latency\n```\n\n### **Filter Stats** (per-filter)\n```\nhttp.{filter_name}.error           # Filter errors\nhttp.{filter_name}.requests        # Requests processed\n```\n\n### **Router Stats** (from Router Filter)\n```\nhttp.router.upstream_rq_total                # Total upstream requests\nhttp.router.upstream_rq_active               # Active upstream requests\nhttp.router.upstream_rq_time_ms              # Upstream latency histogram\nhttp.router.upstream_rq_retry                # Retry attempts\nhttp.router.upstream_rq_time_out             # Upstream timeout\nhttp.router.upstream_rq_reset                # Upstream reset\n```\n\n### **Cluster Stats** (from ClusterManager)\n```\ncluster.{cluster_name}.upstream_cx_total              # Total connections\ncluster.{cluster_name}.upstream_cx_active             # Active connections\ncluster.{cluster_name}.upstream_cx_connect_fail       # Connection failures\ncluster.{cluster_name}.upstream_rq_total              # Total requests\ncluster.{cluster_name}.upstream_rq_active             # Active requests\ncluster.{cluster_name}.upstream_rq_pending            # Queued requests\ncluster.{cluster_name}.upstream_rq_time_out           # Request timeouts\ncluster.{cluster_name}.circuit_breakers_default_cx_open  # Circuit breaker\n```\n\n---\n\n## Key Architectural Patterns\n\n### **1. Lazy Initialization**\n- Codec created only when needed (on first data)\n- Connection pool created on first upstream request to cluster\n- Reduces startup latency and memory usage\n\n### **2. Thread-Local Everything**\n- Thread-local cluster instances\n- Thread-local connection pools per thread\n- No locks needed on hot paths\n\n### **3. Stop-and-Resume Pattern**\n- Filters return `StopIteration` to pause chain\n- Explicitly call `continueDecoding()/continueEncoding()` to resume\n- Enables arbitrary async operations within filter chain\n\n### **4. Bidirectional Filter Chain**\n- Same filters process both request and response\n- Encoder filters iterate in reverse of decoder order\n- Symmetric processing: filter A on request, filter A on response\n\n### **5. Callback-Based Async**\n- Connection pool returns via callbacks (not blocking)\n- Upstream response via `ResponseDecoder` callbacks\n- All I/O non-blocking, event-driven\n\n### **6. Circuit Breaking and Backpressure**\n- Limits prevent resource exhaustion (connections, requests)\n- Watermarks throttle slow consumers\n- Overload detection sheds load\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe HTTP Connection Manager in Envoy is a sophisticated, multi-layered architecture:\n\n1. **ConnectionManagerImpl** — Acts as the bridge between raw TCP bytes and logical HTTP streams, managing codec selection, stream lifecycle, and connection-level concerns.\n\n2. **FilterManager** — Executes a bidirectional filter chain where each filter can intercept and modify requests/responses, with clear control flow semantics for stopping and resuming iteration.\n\n3. **Router Filter** — The terminal decoder filter that selects upstream destinations, obtains connection pools, manages request lifetime, retry logic, and timeouts.\n\n4. **ClusterManager & Upstream Connectivity** — Abstracts upstream clusters and connections, providing load balancing, health checking, and connection pooling across multiple protocols and strategies.\n\nTogether, these components provide a composable, extensible platform for building HTTP proxies and API gateways with sophisticated traffic control, observability, and reliability features.\n\n---\n\n## Relevant Source Files Reference\n\n**Core HTTP Connection Manager:**\n- `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h` — Main implementation\n- `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.cc` — Implementation\n- `source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h` — Configuration\n\n**Filter Chain Execution:**\n- `source/common/http/filter_manager.h` — Filter chain engine\n- `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc` — Implementation\n- `envoy/http/filter.h` — Filter interface definitions\n\n**Router Filter:**\n- `source/common/router/router.cc` — Router implementation\n- `source/common/router/router.h` — Filter interface (in envoy/router/)\n- `source/common/router/config_impl.h` — Route configuration\n- `source/common/router/retry_state_impl.h` — Retry logic\n\n**Codecs:**\n- `source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.h` — HTTP/1.1\n- `source/common/http/http2/codec_impl.h` — HTTP/2\n- `source/common/quic/codec_impl.h` — HTTP/3\n\n**Connection Pools:**\n- `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.h` — Base pool interface\n- `source/common/http/http1/conn_pool.h` — HTTP/1.1 pool\n- `source/common/http/http2/conn_pool.h` — HTTP/2 pool\n- `source/common/http/http3/conn_pool.h` — HTTP/3 pool\n\n**Cluster Manager:**\n- `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h` — Implementation\n- `envoy/upstream/cluster_manager.h` — Interface\n- `envoy/upstream/load_balancer.h` — Load balancer interface\n\n**Configuration & Discovery:**\n- `source/common/router/config_utility.cc` — Route config utilities\n- `envoy/router/rds.h` — Route configuration provider
